(H	)I
     Controller Guide    
       Normal Shot       
     Reflect Barrier     
       Force Bomb        
                                        
                                        
                                        
Push the SHOT button.                   
weapon and shoot projectiles.           
                                        
Hold and release SHOT.                  
Hold the SHOT button and then release it
when the gauge is at MAX.               
Hold and release SHOT.                  
If you use the Reflect Barrier, it can't
be used until the gauge is full again.  
Hold and release SHOT.                  
The Reflect Barrier will reflect the    
enemies' bullets.                       
Hold and release SHOT.                  
You are invincible while the Reflect    
Barrier is active.                      
Push the BOMB button.                   
Push the BOMB button to unleash the     
Force Bomb.                             
Push the BOMB button.                   
The Force Bomb extinguishes enemy       
bullets.
